<a id="1918" class="Keyword">private</a> <a id="1926" class="Keyword">variable</a>  <a id="1936" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1936" class="Generalizable">Î±</a> <a id="1938" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1938" class="Generalizable">Ïáµƒ</a> <a id="1941" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1941" class="Generalizable">Î²</a> <a id="1943" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1943" class="Generalizable">Ïáµ‡</a> <a id="1946" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1946" class="Generalizable">Î³</a> <a id="1948" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1948" class="Generalizable">Ïá¶œ</a> <a id="1951" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1951" class="Generalizable">Î¹</a> <a id="1953" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1955" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a>

Recall, `f ~ g` means f and g are *extensionally* (or pointwise) equal; i.e., `âˆ€ x, f x â‰¡ g x`. We use this notion of equality of functions in the following definition of *isomorphism*.

We could define this using Sigma types, like this.

```agda
_â‰…_ : {Î± Î² : Level}(ğ‘¨ : Algebra Î± ğ‘†)(ğ‘© : Algebra Î² Ïáµ‡) â†’ Type(ğ“ âŠ” ğ“¥ âŠ” Î± âŠ” Î²)
ğ‘¨ â‰… ğ‘© =  Î£[ f âˆˆ (hom ğ‘¨ ğ‘©)] Î£[ g âˆˆ hom ğ‘© ğ‘¨ ] ((âˆ£ f âˆ£ âˆ˜ âˆ£ g âˆ£ â‰ˆ âˆ£ ğ’¾ğ’¹ ğ‘© âˆ£) Ã— (âˆ£ g âˆ£ âˆ˜ âˆ£ f âˆ£ â‰ˆ âˆ£ ğ’¾ğ’¹ ğ‘¨ âˆ£))
```

However, with four components, an equivalent record type is easier to work with.

   <a id="3469" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="3478" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3478" class="Function">Î¾</a> <a id="3480" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3482" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3484" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2797" class="Field">to</a> <a id="3487" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3489" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1878" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3493" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3494" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3496" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2813" class="Field">from</a> <a id="3501" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3503" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1878" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3507" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3449" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3508" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3510" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2675" class="Function Operator">â‰ˆâ‚‚</a> <a id="3513" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3515" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2797" class="Field">to</a> <a id="3518" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3520" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1878" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3524" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3525" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3527" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2813" class="Field">from</a> <a id="3532" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3534" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1878" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="3538" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3453" class="Bound">y</a><a id="3539" class="Symbol">)</a>
   <a id="3544" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3478" class="Function">Î¾</a> <a id="3546" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3548" href="Function.Bundles.html#1938" class="Field">cong</a> <a id="3553" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3555" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2797" class="Field">to</a> <a id="3558" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="3560" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3456" class="Bound">xy</a>
   <a id="3566" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3566" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="3571" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3573" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3449" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="3575" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2675" class="Function Operator">â‰ˆâ‚‚</a> <a id="3578" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3453" class="Bound">y</a>
   <a id="3583" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3566" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="3588" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3590" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2705" class="Function">transâ‚‚</a> <a id="3597" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3598" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2689" class="Function">symâ‚‚</a> <a id="3603" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3604" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2831" class="Field">toâˆ¼from</a> <a id="3612" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3449" class="Bound">x</a><a id="3613" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="3616" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3617" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2705" class="Function">transâ‚‚</a> <a id="3624" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3478" class="Function">Î¾</a> <a id="3626" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3627" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2831" class="Field">toâˆ¼from</a> <a id="3635" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3453" class="Bound">y</a><a id="3636" class="Symbol">))</a>

</pre>

That is, two structures are *isomorphic* provided there are homomorphisms going back and forth between them which compose to the identity map.


#### <a id="properties-of-isomorphisms-of-setoid-algebras">Properties of isomorphism of setoid algebras</a>

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3920" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="3925" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2722" class="Module Operator">_â‰…_</a>

  <a id="5041" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="5049" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5049" class="Function">lem1</a> <a id="5054" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5056" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5019" class="Bound">aâ‚€</a> <a id="5059" href="Relation.Binary.Bundles.html#1098" class="Function Operator">â‰ˆ</a> <a id="5061" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5062" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5005" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="5064" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1878" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="5068" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5069" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4997" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="5071" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1878" class="Field Operator">âŸ¨$âŸ©</a> <a id="5075" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5019" class="Bound">aâ‚€</a><a id="5077" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="5153" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5104" class="Function">lem2</a> <a id="5158" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5160" href="Function.Bundles.html#1938" class="Field">cong</a> <a id="5165" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5005" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="5167" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5027" class="Bound">fafb</a>

  <a id="5240" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5223" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="5245" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5247" href="Relation.Binary.Structures.html#1620" class="Function">trans</a> <a id="5253" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5049" class="Function">lem1</a> <a id="5258" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5259" href="Relation.Binary.Structures.html#1620" class="Function">trans</a> <a id="5265" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5104" class="Function">lem2</a> <a id="5270" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5174" class="Function">lem3</a><a id="5274" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="5278" class="Comment">-- The &quot;from&quot; map of an isomorphism is injective.</a>
<a id="â‰…fromInjective"></a><a id="5328" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5328" class="Function">â‰…fromInjective</a> <a id="5343" class="Symbol">:</a>  <a id="5346" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5347" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5347" class="Bound">ğ‘¨</a> <a id="5349" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5351" href="Setoid.Algebras.Basic.html#2837" class="Record">Algebra</a> <a id="5359" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1936" class="Generalizable">Î±</a> <a id="5361" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1938" class="Generalizable">Ïáµƒ</a><a id="5363" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5365" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5365" class="Bound">ğ‘©</a> <a id="5367" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5369" href="Setoid.Algebras.Basic.html#2837" class="Record">Algebra</a> <a id="5377" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1941" class="Generalizable">Î²</a> <a id="5379" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1943" class="Generalizable">Ïáµ‡</a><a id="5381" class="Symbol">}</a>
                  <a id="5401" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5402" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5402" class="Bound">Ï†</a> <a id="5404" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5406" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5347" class="Bound">ğ‘¨</a> <a id="5408" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2722" class="Record Operator">â‰…</a> <a id="5410" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5365" class="Bound">ğ‘©</a><a id="5411" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5413" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="5415" href="Setoid.Functions.Injective.html#2164" class="Function">IsInjective</a> <a id="5427" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a> <a id="5429" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2813" class="Field">from</a> <a id="5434" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5402" class="Bound">Ï†</a> <a id="5436" href="Overture.Basic.html#4326" class="Function Operator">âˆ£</a>

<a id="5439" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5328" class="Function">â‰…fromInjective</a> <a id="5454" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5454" class="Bound">Ï†</a> <a id="5456" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5458" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4925" class="Function">â‰…toInjective</a> <a id="5471" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5472" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4065" class="Function">â‰…-sym</a> <a id="5478" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5454" class="Bound">Ï†</a><a id="5479" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

Fortunately, the lift operation preserves isomorphism (i.e., it's an *algebraic
invariant*). As our focus is universal algebra, this is important and is what
makes the lift operation a workable solution to the technical problems that arise
from the noncumulativity of Agda's universe hierarchy.

<pre class="Agda">

           <a id="6758" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6759" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6367" class="Function">Lift-Alg-isoÊ³</a> <a id="6773" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5850" class="Function">Lift-â‰…Ë¡</a><a id="6780" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

The lift is also associative, up to isomorphism at least.

 <a id="7420" class="Symbol">â†’</a>             <a id="7434" href="Setoid.Algebras.Basic.html#5877" class="Function">Lift-Alg</a> <a id="7443" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7389" class="Bound">ğ‘¨</a> <a id="7445" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7446" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7406" class="Bound">Î²</a> <a id="7448" href="Agda.Primitive.html#810" class="Primitive Operator">âŠ”</a> <a id="7450" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7408" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="7451" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7453" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7454" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7406" class="Bound">Î²</a> <a id="7456" href="Agda.Primitive.html#810" class="Primitive Operator">âŠ”</a> <a id="7458" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7408" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="7459" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7461" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2722" class="Record Operator">â‰…</a> <a id="7463" href="Setoid.Algebras.Basic.html#5877" class="Function">Lift-Alg</a> <a id="7472" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7473" href="Setoid.Algebras.Basic.html#5877" class="Function">Lift-Alg</a> <a id="7482" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7389" class="Bound">ğ‘¨</a> <a id="7484" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7406" class="Bound">Î²</a> <a id="7486" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7406" class="Bound">Î²</a><a id="7487" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7489" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7408" class="Bound">Î³</a> <a id="7491" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7408" class="Bound">Î³</a>
<a id="7493" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7373" class="Function">Lift-assoc&#39;</a><a id="7504" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7505" class="Argument">ğ‘¨</a> <a id="7507" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7509" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7509" class="Bound">ğ‘¨</a><a id="7510" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7512" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7512" class="Bound">Î²</a><a id="7513" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7515" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7515" class="Bound">Î³</a><a id="7516" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7518" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7520" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4160" class="Function">â‰…-trans</a> <a id="7528" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7529" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4065" class="Function">â‰…-sym</a> <a id="7535" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6073" class="Function">Lift-â‰…</a><a id="7541" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7543" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7544" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4160" class="Function">â‰…-trans</a> <a id="7552" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6073" class="Function">Lift-â‰…</a> <a id="7559" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6073" class="Function">Lift-â‰…</a><a id="7565" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

Products of isomorphic families of algebras are themselves isomorphic. The proof
looks a bit technical, but it is as straightforward as it ought to be.

<pre class="Agda">

   <a id="8762" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8724" class="Function">Ïˆâˆ¼Ï•</a> <a id="8766" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8766" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8768" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8770" class="Symbol">Î»</a> <a id="8772" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8772" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="8774" class="Symbol">â†’</a> <a id="8776" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2885" class="Field">fromâˆ¼to</a> <a id="8784" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8785" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8111" class="Bound">AB</a> <a id="8788" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8772" class="Bound">i</a><a id="8789" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8791" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8766" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8793" href="Setoid.Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#8772" class="Bound">i</a><a id="8794" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

A nearly identical proof goes through for isomorphisms of lifted products.

<pre class="Agda">
